pneumoniae circulation," NSW Health said.</span></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>"Such increases usually occur every three to seven years as population immunity wanes.</span></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>"While the majority of childhood pneumonias are caused by a variety of viruses and bacterial infections, the proportion of presentations and admissions due to mycoplasma pneumonia and atypical pneumonia is starting to increase."</span></div></div><div><div class="OUTBRAIN" data-src="//www.9news.com.au/national/mycoplasma-pneumonia-what-is-it-signs-symptoms-causes-everything-to-know-explainer/1407476a-4244-4eb7-aa4f-76f8afc40231" data-widget-id="AR_5" data-reactroot=""></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><h3><span>What is Mycoplasma pneumonia?</span></h3></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>Pneumonia is an infection of the lungs.</span></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>The infection is usually caused by bacteria or a virus, </span><a href="https://www.healthdirect.gov.au/pneumonia" target="" rel="" title=" Health Direct says."><span>Health Direct says.</span></a></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>One of the most common and deadly types is pneumococcal pneumonia, which is caused by the bacterium Streptococcus pneumoniae, according to the Lung Foundation.</span></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>Mycoplasma pneumonia is another type of pneumonia and is caused by the bacteria mycoplasma pneumoniae.</span></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>Pneumonia caused by mycoplasma organisms is generally mild, but recovery takes longer, the Lung Foundation said.</span></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>It spreads through contact with an infected person, such as when they cough or sneeze.</span></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><strong><span>READ MORE:</span></strong><span> </span><a href="https://www.9news.com.au/health/covid-rsv-flu-influenza-common-cold-symptoms-at-risk-groups-treatments-prevention-explained/8e7fa278-2f2b-41c3-9413-864914e566c2" target="" rel="" title="How do I know whether I have a cold, COVID-19, RSV or flu?﻿"><strong><span>How do I know whether I have a cold, COVID-19, RSV or flu?﻿</span></strong></a></div></div><figure class="article__image"><img src="https://imageresizer.static9.net.au/qt-krNdg8blFVIoAMSmDj_XCgL8=/500x0/https%3A%2F%2Fprod.static9.net.au%2Ffs%2Fd13f6e86-84ac-4681-835e-a01a85343b16" srcset="https://imageresizer.static9.net.au/qt-krNdg8blFVIoAMSmDj_XCgL8=/500x0/https%3A%2F%2Fprod.static9.net.au%2Ffs%2Fd13f6e86-84ac-4681-835e-a01a85343b16 500w, https://imageresizer.static9.net.au/0OGTBYEVFG7bPHtvT3FwmWTj0bU=/600x0/https%3A%2F%2Fprod.static9.net.au%2Ffs%2Fd13f6e86-84ac-4681-835e-a01a85343b16 600w, https://imageresizer.static9.net.au/tWvDOgbAj3LMrLj27YRNHIcjpUY=/800x0/https%3A%2F%2Fprod.static9.net.au%2Ffs%2Fd13f6e86-84ac-4681-835e-a01a85343b16 800w, https://imageresizer.static9.net.au/LWpAObgEhABBjnIsaFTPIlmNMzE=/1000x0/https%3A%2F%2Fprod.static9.net.au%2Ffs%2Fd13f6e86-84ac-4681-835e-a01a85343b16 1000w, (min-width: 768px) 600px, 500px" alt=""><figcaption class="article__caption">Mycoplasma pneumonia is another type of pneumonia and is caused by the bacteria mycoplasma pneumoniae.<!-- --> <!-- -->(Jessica Hromas)</figcaption></figure><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><h3><span>Signs and symptoms of Mycoplasma pneumonia</span></h3></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>Symptoms may develop over one to three weeks.</span></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>Like other respiratory diseases, they include fever, a dry cough, headache, sore throat, and a general feeling of being unwell.</span></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>The cough may last for more than a month, alongside feeling lethargic, NSW Health said.</span></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>This type of pneumonia can also have some different symptoms such as white phlegm, nausea and vomiting, the Lung Foundation said.</span></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>Doctors are being warned cases of this type of the disease can appear mild compared with other kinds of pneumonia, which are more likely to kill.</span></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>"People with Mycoplasma pneumonia may appear well, often referred to as 'walking pneumonia," NSW Health said.</span></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>A chest X-Ray, blood and PCR tests are among methods of diagnosis.</span></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><strong><span>READ MORE: ﻿</span></strong><a href="https://www.9news.com.au/national/covid19-update-what-need-know-current-rules-latest-symptoms-explainer/2b26f37b-4d16-46d4-8280-a99eeb54f9e1"><strong><span>Do I need to age groups aged five to 20 years but can happen at any age.</span></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><em><span>Mycoplasma pneumoniae</span></em><span> causes 15 to 50 per cent of cases of pneumonia in adults and an even higher percentage in school aged children, according to SA Health.</span></div></div><div treated﻿?</span></h3></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>While often no treatment is needed for the illness to resolve on its own,
